</tr><tr><td class="sidebar-navbar"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1129693374"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1239400231">.mw-parser-output .navbar{display:inline;font-size:88%;font-weight:normal}.mw-parser-output .navbar-collapse{float:left;text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .navbar-boxtext{word-spacing:0}.mw-parser-output .navbar ul{display:inline-block;white-space:nowrap;line-height:inherit}.mw-parser-output .navbar-brackets::before{margin-right:-0.125em;content:"[ "}.mw-parser-output .navbar-brackets::after{margin-left:-0.125em;content:" ]"}.mw-parser-output .navbar li{word-spacing:-0.125em}.mw-parser-output .navbar a>span,.mw-parser-output .navbar a>abbr{text-decoration:inherit}.mw-parser-output .navbar-mini abbr{font-variant:small-caps;border-bottom:none;text-decoration:none;cursor:inherit}.mw-parser-output .navbar-ct-full{font-size:114%;margin:0 7em}.mw-parser-output .navbar-ct-mini{font-size:114%;margin:0 4em}html.skin-theme-clientpref-night .mw-parser-output .navbar li a abbr{color:var(--color-base)!important}@media(prefers-color-scheme:dark){html.skin-theme-clientpref-os .mw-parser-output .navbar li a abbr{color:var(--color-base)!important}}@media print{.mw-parser-output .navbar{display:none!important}}</style><div class="navbar plainlinks hlist navbar-mini"><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Template:Machine_learning" title="Template:Machine learning"><abbr title="View this template">v</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Template_talk:Machine_learning" title="Template talk:Machine learning"><abbr title="Discuss this template">t</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Special:EditPage/Template:Machine_learning" title="Special:EditPage/Template:Machine learning"><abbr title="Edit this template">e</abbr></a></li></ul></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>IBM Granite</b> is a series of decoder-only <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/AI" class="mw-redirect" title="AI">AI</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Foundation_model" title="Foundation model">foundation models</a> created by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM" title="IBM">IBM</a>. It was announced on September 7, 2023,<sup id="cite_ref-auto1_3-0" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-auto1-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> and an initial paper was published 4 days later.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-5"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>5<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Initially intended for use in the IBM's <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cloud-based" class="mw-redirect" title="Cloud-based">cloud-based</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data" title="Data">data</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Generative_AI" class="mw-redirect" title="Generative AI">generative AI</a> platform <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Watsonx" class="mw-redirect" title="Watsonx">Watsonx</a> along with other models,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-6"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>6<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> IBM opened the source code of some code models.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-7"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>7<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Granite models are trained on datasets curated from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet" title="Internet">Internet</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academic_publishing" title="Academic publishing">academic publishings</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Source_code" title="Source code">code</a> datasets, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Legal_instrument" title="Legal instrument">legal</a> and finance documents.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-8"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>8<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-9"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>9<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-auto_1-1" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-auto-1"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>1<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc">
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Foundation_models">Foundation models</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=IBM_Granite&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Foundation models"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>A foundation model is an AI model trained on broad data at scale such that it can be adapted to a wide range of downstream tasks.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-10"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>10<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>Granite's first foundation models were Granite.13b.instruct and Granite.13b.chat. The "13b" in their name comes from 13 billion, the amount of parameters they have as models, lesser than most of the larger models of the time.  Later models vary from 3 to 34 billion parameters.<sup id="cite_ref-auto1_3-1" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-auto1-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-11"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>11<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On May 6, 2024, IBM released the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Source_code" title="Source code">source code</a> of four variations of Granite Code Models under <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Apache_License" title="Apache License">Apache 2</a>, an open source <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Permissive_software_license" title="Permissive software license">permissive license</a> that allows completely free use, modification and sharing of the software, and put them on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hugging_Face" title="Hugging Face">Hugging Face</a> for public use.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-12"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>12<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-13"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>13<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> According to IBM's own report, Granite 8b outperforms <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Llama_3" class="mw-redirect" title="Llama 3">Llama 3</a> on several <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_programming" title="Computer programming">coding</a> related tasks within similar range of parameters.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-14"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>14<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IBM_Granite?utm_source=ibm_developer&amp;utm_content=in_content_link&amp;utm_id=tutorials_awb-contributing-llm-granite-instructlab-ui#cite_note-15"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>15<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
